</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id11_a2d4ce-80 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column11_b48694-e8"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p class="kt-adv-heading11_2c069d-d2 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading11_2c069d-d2">Hi, we’re Anna and Anne – two German natives, a married couple, and passionate travelers living in Germany.</p>



<p>After years of traveling the world, we realized how many visitors miss out on the truly special sides of Germany — the cozy towns, scenic train routes, and local traditions that make it unique.</p>



<p>That’s why we created <strong>Germany Things To Do</strong>: a travel blog about Germany made for first-time visitors who want to experience Germany beyond the clichés. Here you’ll find honest guides, practical travel tips, and local insights to help you plan your first trip!</p>



<p>Whether you’re coming for a short visit, a semester abroad, or thinking about moving to Germany — we’ll help you discover what makes this country so worth exploring.</p>
